    SELECT TOP(1) [r].[Id], [r].[Address], [r].[AverageDeliveryTimeMinutes], [r].[AverageRating], [r].[BannerUrl], [r].[City], [r].[CreatedAt], [r].[CuisineType], [r].[Description], [r].[Email], [r].[IsOpen], [r].[Latitude], [r].[LogoUrl], [r].[Longitude], [r].[MinimumOrderAmount], [r].[Name], [r].[OwnerId], [r].[PhoneNumber], [r].[PinCode], [r].[Status], [r].[TotalRatings], [r].[UpdatedAt]

) AS [t]

    FROM [MenuCategories] AS [m]
    LEFT JOIN [MenuItems] AS [m0] ON [m].[Id] = [m0].[CategoryId]
) AS [t0] ON [t].[Id] = [t0].[RestaurantId]
LEFT JOIN [RestaurantHours] AS [r0] ON [t].[Id] = [r0].[RestaurantId]
